			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'b5c0eb86a666fab6f9b36f88aa12f9dd3fd40198') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '77b7d41bc4d6e28ff026cc47a075415fe8c65362') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '77b7d41bc4d6e28ff026cc47a075415fe8c65362') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'f851599b26e419247163dc0dd5aaf643db174d36') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '77b7d41bc4d6e28ff026cc47a075415fe8c65362') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php') !== 'c6477fe30f0326925dd62cbf94eed1ddb360298d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '5d84eb4fb1194467c6c6f7a069e5eeff62626828') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5d84eb4fb1194467c6c6f7a069e5eeff62626828') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '907556fdb3e933247383b3b67ab61acfd6d6161a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5d84eb4fb1194467c6c6f7a069e5eeff62626828') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js') != 'da75ce2d47cc2e70a1cbf2a33af3cb96215c146e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js') !== 'da75ce2d47cc2e70a1cbf2a33af3cb96215c146e') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js') !== '7767faf4296314f0fd271200ee0815a4e62716ec') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js') !== 'da75ce2d47cc2e70a1cbf2a33af3cb96215c146e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/OIDplusPagePublicLogin.js');
		}
	}
